describes the active authentication architecture.\n\n## Active Flows\n\n- Password auth (username/email + password)\n- Google OAuth login\n- Google account linking/unlinking from an authenticated profile\n\nEmail verification code remains in the repository for future re-enable, but it is not part of the active flow.\n\n## Base Path\n\n`/api/v1/auth`\n\n## Endpoints\n\n### 1) `GET /csrf-token`\nReturns an anonymous CSRF token and sets `anon_csrf` cookie.\n\n### 2) `POST /register`\nCreates a user account (does not auto-login).\n\nRequest body:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"username\": \"pilotname\",\n  \"email\": \"player@example.com\",\n  \"password\": \"StrongPass123\"\n}\n```\n\nResponse:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"message\": \"User registered successfully\",\n  \"user\": {\n \"updated_at\": \"...\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 3) `POST /login`\nLogs in with `identifier` (username or email) + password.\nSets access/refresh JWT cookies and CSRF cookies.\n\n### 4) `GET /google/login`\nStarts Google OAuth login redirect flow.\n\n### 5) `GET /google/callback`\nHandles OAuth callback, creates or links account, issues JWT cookies, redirects to frontend.\n\n### 6) `POST /google/link/start`\nAuthenticated endpoint to begin linking a Google account to the current user.\n\n### 7) `POST /google/unlink`\nAuthenticated endpoint to unlink the currently linked Google account.\n\n### 8) `GET /me`\nReturns current authenticated user profile.\n\n### 9) `PATCH /me/username`\nUpdates the in-game username for the authenticated user.\n\n### 10) `POST /refresh`\nRefreshes access token using refresh token cookie + refresh CSRF token.\n\n### 11) `POST /logout`\nClears auth and CSRF cookies.\n\n## Environment Variables (Auth)\n\nRequired:\n- `SECRET_KEY`\n- `JWT_SECRET_KEY`\n\nGoogle OAuth:\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`\n- `BACKEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `FRONTEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `GOOGLE_OAUTH_REDIRECT_PATH`\n- Requires a valid access JWT cookie, but no\nCSRF header. Returns the current authenticated CSRF cookie values:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"csrf_access_token\": \"...\",\n  \"csrf_refresh_token\": \"...\",\n  \"anon_csrf\": \"\"\n}\n```\n\nMalformed, expired, wrong-type, or otherwise rejected access JWT cookies return\nthe standard invalid-token response: `\"Invalid or expired token\"`.\n\n### 3) `POST /register`\nCreates a user account (does not auto-login).\nRequires `X-CSRF-TOKEN` matching the `anon_csrf` cookie. Missing or mismatched\nanonymous CSRF values return `\"Invalid or missing CSRF token\"`.\n\nRequest body:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"username\": \"pilotname\",\n  \"email\": \"player@example.com\",\n  \"password\": \"StrongPass123\"\n}\n```\n\nResponse:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"message\": \"User registered successfully\",\n  \"user\": {\n    \"_id\": \"...\",\n    \"username\": \"pilotname\",\n    \"email\": \"player@example.com\",\n    \"google_email\": null,\n    \"google_linked\": false,\n    \"created_at\": \"...\",\n    \"updated_at\": \"...\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n### 4) `POST /login`\nLogs in with `identifier` (username or email) + password.\nSets access/refresh JWT cookies and CSRF cookies.\nRequires `X-CSRF-TOKEN` matching the `anon_csrf` cookie. On success, the\nanonymous CSRF cookie is cleared.\n\n### 5) `GET /google/login`\nStarts Google OAuth login redirect flow.\n\n### 6) `GET /google/callback`\nHandles OAuth callback, creates or links account, issues JWT cookies, redirects to frontend.\nOn successful login, the anonymous CSRF cookie is cleared.\n\n### 7) `POST /google/link/start`\nAuthenticated endpoint to begin linking a Google account to the current user.\n\n### 8) `POST /google/unlink`\nAuthenticated endpoint to unlink the currently linked Google account.\n\n### 9) `GET /me`\nReturns current authenticated user profile.\n\n### 10) `PATCH /me/username`\nUpdates the in-game username for the authenticated user.\n\n### 11) `POST /refresh`\nRefreshes access token using refresh token cookie + refresh CSRF token.\n\n### 12) `POST /logout`\nClears auth and CSRF cookies.\nRequires access token cookie + `X-CSRF-TOKEN` matching `csrf_access_token`.\nAuthenticated-token failures, including missing or mismatched authenticated CSRF,\nreturn the standard invalid-token response.\n\n## Environment Variables (Auth)\n\nRequired:\n- `SECRET_KEY`\n- `JWT_SECRET_KEY`\n\nGoogle OAuth:\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_ID`\n- `GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET`\n- `BACKEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `FRONTEND_PUBLIC_BASE_URL`\n- `GOOGLE_OAUTH_REDIRECT_PATH`\n- `FRONTEND_OAUTH_SUCCESS_PATH`\n- `FRONTEND_OAUTH_FAILURE_PATH`\n- `FRONTEND_OAUTH_LINK_SUCCESS_PATH`\n- `FRONTEND_OAUTH_LINK_FAILURE_PATH`\n\nOptional:\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}
